   <script>
    jQuery(document).ready(function(){
		if( Modernizr.cookies ){
			jQuery.cookie('060-cookies', 'true', { expires: 365, path: '/' });
		} else {
			jQuery.cookie('060-cookies', 'false', { expires: 365, path: '/' });
		}
	});
	
	jQuery( document ).on( 'click', 'span.compareCar', function() {
		var $this = jQuery(this);

		var carID = $this.data('stat-id');
		var carName = $this.data('stat-name');
		
		var carCount = $.cookie('060-compare-cars-c');
		
		var cookiesEnabled = $.cookie('060-cookies');
		
		if(cookiesEnabled == 'true'){ 
			if(!carCount){
				jQuery('div.compareAlert').text(carName+' has been selected for comparison!');
				jQuery('div.compareAlert').fadeIn();
			}
			
			if(carCount == 0){
				jQuery('div.compareAlert').text(carName+' has been selected for comparison!');
				jQuery('div.compareAlert').fadeIn();
			}
			
			if(carCount &lt; 12){
				jQuery('div.compareAlert').text(carName+' has been selected for comparison!');
				jQuery('div.compareAlert').fadeIn();
			}
			
			if(carCount == 12){
				jQuery('div.compareAlert').text("You can't select more than 12 cars to compare. Please visit the Compare Cars page to manage your selections!");
				jQuery('div.compareAlert').fadeIn();
			}
		} 
		
		if(cookiesEnabled != 'true'){ 
			jQuery('div.compareAlert').addClass('error').text('This feature only works if cookies are enabled!');
			jQuery('div.compareAlert').fadeIn();
		}

		function hideAlert() { 
			jQuery('div.compareAlert').fadeOut('slow');
			jQuery('div.compareAlert').removeClass('error');
		}
		
		window.setTimeout(hideAlert, 3000);

		if(!carCount){
			carCount = 1;
			jQuery.cookie('060-compare-cars-c', carCount, { expires: 365, path: '/' });
			jQuery.cookie('060-compare-cars-1', carID, { expires: 365, path: '/' });
			return;
		}
		
		if(carCount == 0){
			carCount = 1;
			jQuery.cookie('060-compare-cars-c', carCount, { expires: 365, path: '/' });
			jQuery.cookie('060-compare-cars-1', carID, { expires: 365, path: '/' });
			return;
		}
		
		if(carCount == 1){
			carCount = 2;
			jQuery.cookie('060-compare-cars-c', carCount, { expires: 365, path: '/' });
			jQuery.cookie('060-compare-cars-2', carID, { expires: 365, path: '/' });
			return;
		}
		if(carCount == 2){
			carCount = 3;
			jQuery.cookie('060-compare-cars-c', carCount, { expires: 365, path: '/' });
			jQuery.cookie('060-compare-cars-3', carID, { expires: 365, path: '/' });
			return;
		}
		if(carCount == 3){
			carCount = 4;
			jQuery.cookie('060-compare-cars-c', carCount, { expires: 365, path: '/' });
			jQuery.cookie('060-compare-cars-4', carID, { expires: 365, path: '/' });
			return;
		}
		
		if(carCount == 4){
			carCount = 5;
			jQuery.cookie('060-compare-cars-c', carCount, { expires: 365, path: '/' });
			jQuery.cookie('060-compare-cars-5', carID, { expires: 365, path: '/' });
			return;
		}
		
		if(carCount == 5){
			carCount = 6;
			jQuery.cookie('060-compare-cars-c', carCount, { expires: 365, path: '/' });
			jQuery.cookie('060-compare-cars-6', carID, { expires: 365, path: '/' });
			return;
		}
		
		if(carCount == 6){
			carCount = 7;
			jQuery.cookie('060-compare-cars-c', carCount, { expires: 365, path: '/' });
			jQuery.cookie('060-compare-cars-7', carID, { expires: 365, path: '/' });
			return;
		}
		
		if(carCount == 7){
			carCount = 8;
			jQuery.cookie('060-compare-cars-c', carCount, { expires: 365, path: '/' });
			jQuery.cookie('060-compare-cars-8', carID, { expires: 365, path: '/' });
			return;
		}
		
		if(carCount == 8){
			carCount = 9;
			jQuery.cookie('060-compare-cars-c', carCount, { expires: 365, path: '/' });
			jQuery.cookie('060-compare-cars-9', carID, { expires: 365, path: '/' });
			return;
		}
		
		if(carCount == 9){
			carCount = 10;
			jQuery.cookie('060-compare-cars-c', carCount, { expires: 365, path: '/' });
			jQuery.cookie('060-compare-cars-10', carID, { expires: 365, path: '/' });
			return;
		}
		
		if(carCount == 10){
			carCount = 11;
			jQuery.cookie('060-compare-cars-c', carCount, { expires: 365, path: '/' });
			jQuery.cookie('060-compare-cars-11', carID, { expires: 365, path: '/' });
			return;
		}
		
		if(carCount == 11){
			carCount = 12;
			jQuery.cookie('060-compare-cars-c', carCount, { expires: 365, path: '/' });
			jQuery.cookie('060-compare-cars-12', carID, { expires: 365, path: '/' });
			return;
		}
		
	});
   </script>

      <article class="post-72308 cbd_stats type-cbd_stats status-publish hentry vehicle-make-mclaren-0-60-mph-times body-style-coupe body-style-supercar-hypercar" id="post-72308" role="article">
       <h1 class="entry-title">
        Supercar 0-60 Times
       </h1>
       <div class="entry-content">
        <div class="vehicleStyleContent">
         <img alt="Supercar 0 to 60 Times" src="//www.zeroto60times.com/wp-content/uploads/2014/05/Supercar1.png"/>
         <h2>
          List of Supercar performance specs
         </h2>
         <p>
          If youre wondering just how fast a supercar really is then youre in the right place! Find 0-60 mph and quarter mile times for hundreds of old and new supercars from a variety of exotic car manufacturers. Although the definition of a supercar is widely debated among automobile enthusiasts, the cars included in this supercar category are limited to only rare high-performance cars. Hypercars are also included in this section since the term supercar can be used essentially as a catchall that encompasses these top-end exotic cars. Browse by make below to start finding supercar 0-60 and quarter mile stats. Make sure to check back soon for updates to this super car 0 to 60 specs category.
         </p>
        </div>
